msg:The things I am not satisfied with about Jinan Kempinski are: first, it may be that I did not check in at 2 o'clock according to the hotel regulations, or it may be that due to the high check-in rate during the peak season, I was told at 1 o'clock that the room was not cleaned in time, and the booked room was not available for the time being. I need to wait for the cleaning before I can check in. This is understandable. After asking how long I need to wait, I patiently spent time in the lobby and looked at the scenery. As a landmark building in Jinan, the location of Kempinski is indeed remarkable, so the waiting is not so boring, and the scenery outside the window is still good. After waiting for nearly 20 minutes, I thought I could check in to the room normally and rest. After all, it was almost 1:30 in the afternoon, and I was really hungry and tired from running all the way. To be honest, I really wanted to go to eat and then go to the room to sleep. The lobby service staff said that there was still no room, because they had not yet planned to clean it. If they needed to wait, they would have to wait for another half an hour? Then they proposed that they could provide a smoking room as a solution? To be honest, this solution really makes people speechless! After all, at the first check-in, I was told that the room I booked was not available, and there were only smoking rooms of the same type. When I asked whether I was willing to check in, I had clearly stated that I was with my child and was allergic to smoke, which might make him sick, so I didn't want to stay in a smoking room. Only then did I wait in the lobby for 20 minutes. Seeing that my tired family had to wait for a while, I immediately asked to store my luggage, and I and my family went to eat first, and then came to check in. The front desk promised that the luggage could be stored and would help deliver it to the room after the room was cleaned. After an hour after dinner, I returned to the hotel. The hotel did deliver the luggage to the room this time and upgraded the floor. I am very grateful for this. But after checking in, there were still some unsatisfactory aspects. The room smelled of smoke, especially the bathroom, which was the worst hit area of ‚Äã‚Äãsmoke. It may be that other guests did not abide by the hotel regulations and smoked privately. But to a certain extent, it also reflects the problem of incomplete cleaning and incomplete deodorization. And unfortunately, the child had a fever that night! And I couldn't buy medicine at all in the middle of the night. I really have nothing to say!
Second: The internal phone call to the room service was not answered for a long time, and the call to the front desk was not answered until it rang. This service awareness is really sigh-worthy. When checking in, seeing that we were with a young child, there was no service awareness to actively ask whether children's slippers and toiletries were needed. As an old five-star hotel, it can be said that it is a bit speechless.
Third, as a newly built five-star hotel, I can't understand why the water flow in the shower is so small! Really, this bath... You can clearly count the number of water drops. I once wondered if the pipe was blocked? Or is this a new water-saving method of the hotel?
This experience greatly reduced my good impression of Kempinski.

[About location]: The hotel is located at No. 7000 Jingshi Road, Hanyu Jingu, High-tech Zone. Yunding Building is a landmark building in Quancheng. Kempinski‚Äôs sky lobby is located on the 52nd floor of Yunding Building. Floors 52-71 are accommodation, gyms, and self-service Restaurants, etc., when you are in the hotel, you feel like you are stepping on the clouds, and you can enjoy the beautiful scenery of Quancheng.
[About parking]: The hotel parking lot is at No. 1 Yunding Building
Parking lot B2 (3rd floor underground)
Follow the directions in the parking lot to enter the hotel's exclusive parking lot.
(After entering through Gate 1, turn right)
After parking the car, take the hotel elevator to the first floor of the hotel, then take the elevator to the hotel front desk in the sky lobby on the 52nd floor to check in.
[About service and reservation]: In the past, I informed the staff that I wanted to book a room through Dianping.com, and then a staff member would tell you the reservation phone number, and a staff member would book a room for you in time.
